{
   GROUP EXTERNAL_RCV
   INTERNAL
   {
      TYPE      рхо
      MINIMUM    0
      UNIT      едхмхжю
   }

      TYPE      рхо
      MINIMUM    0
      UNIT      едхмхжю
      EDH S7
      LOCATION PLC01:юдпея L1 GroupName хлъ цпсоош
   }
}

   }

!2 = мхг)
POINT  ACT_C3_HOODPOS
{
   GROUP EXTERNAL_RCV
   INTERNAL
   {
      TYPE      ярюрся
      MINIMUM    0
      MAXIMUM    2
      UNIT      FLAG
   }
   EXTERNAL
   {
      TYPE      ярюрся
      MINIMUM    0
      MAXIMUM    2
      UNIT      FLAG
      EDH S7
      LOCATION PLC33:DB2,W44 GroupName ACT_C3_HOODPOS
   }
}
